**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org

```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Agentic Correctness: Implement Firefox XPCOM Component

## Your Task

Write an XPCOM component header and implementation following Firefox's established patterns. Your component must: 1. Use the `NS_DECL_ISUPPORTS` and `NS_DECL_NSIOBSERVERSERVICE` macros as seen in existing components. 2. Implement `QueryInterface`, `AddRef`, `Release` following the reference counting pattern. 3. Register using `NS_GENERIC_FACTORY_CONSTRUCTOR` as found in existing component registrations under `toolkit/components/`. Write your files to `/workspace/`. Also write `/workspace/answer.json` listing the Firefox source files you referenced.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?
- **Keyword presence**: Are required terms present in your explanation?

Perfect! I've successfully created an XPCOM component implementation for Firefox. Here's what I've delivered:

## Files Created

### 1. **nsMyComponent.h** - Component Header
- Uses `NS_DECL_ISUPPORTS` and `NS_DECL_NSIOBSERVERSERVICE` macros (as required)
- Declares `QueryInterface`, `AddRef`, `Release` through the macros
- Includes a static `Create` method following the nsObserverService pattern
- Defines the component CID

### 2. **nsMyComponent.cpp** - Component Implementation
- Uses `NS_IMPL_ISUPPORTS` macro which expands to implement the three reference counting methods:
  - `NS_IMPL_ADDREF` - increments reference count
  - `NS_IMPL_RELEASE` - decrements and deletes on zero
  - `NS_IMPL_QUERY_INTERFACE` - interface discovery
- Implements the `Create` method that instantiates the component and calls `QueryInterface`
- Provides stub implementations of `nsIObserverService` methods

### 3. **nsMyComponentModule.cpp** - Component Registration
- Uses `NS_GENERIC_FACTORY_CONSTRUCTOR` macro to generate the constructor function
- Registers the component with its CID
- Maps the contract ID for service discovery
- Follows Firefox's `mozilla::Module` registration structure

### 4. **answer.json** - Reference Documentation
Documents all referenced Firefox source files from:
- **xpcom/ds/nsObserverService.h/cpp** - canonical observer service implementation
- **xpcom/base/nsISupportsImpl.h** - macro definitions for NS_DECL_ISUPPORTS, NS_IMPL_ISUPPORTS, AddRef/Release
- **xpcom/components/ModuleUtils.h** - NS_GENERIC_FACTORY_CONSTRUCTOR macro definitions
- **toolkit/components/alerts/nsAlertsService.h/cpp** - component pattern example
- **netwerk/build/nsNetModule.cpp** - registration pattern with NS_GENERIC_FACTORY_CONSTRUCTOR

#ifndef nsMyComponent_h_
#define nsMyComponent_h_

#include "nsIObserverService.h"
#include "nsISupports.h"

// {D07F5195-E3D1-11d2-8ACD-00105A1B8860}
#define NS_MYCOMPONENT_CID \
  {0xd07f5195, 0xe3d1, 0x11d2, {0x8a, 0xcd, 0x0, 0x10, 0x5a, 0x1b, 0x88, 0x60}}

class nsMyComponent final : public nsIObserverService {
 public:
  NS_INLINE_DECL_STATIC_IID(NS_MYCOMPONENT_CID)

  nsMyComponent();

  NS_DECL_ISUPPORTS
  NS_DECL_NSIOBSERVERSERVICE

  [[nodiscard]] static nsresult Create(const nsIID& aIID, void** aInstancePtr);

 private:
  ~nsMyComponent(void);
};

#endif /* nsMyComponent_h_ */

/* This Source Code Form is subject to the terms of the Mozilla Public

 * file, You can obtain one at http://mozilla.org/MPL/2.0/. */

#include "nsMyComponent.h"
#include "nsIObserver.h"
#include "nsISupports.h"
#include "nsComponentManagerUtils.h"
#include "nsServiceManagerUtils.h"

// Implementation of nsISupports methods
NS_IMPL_ISUPPORTS(nsMyComponent, nsIObserverService)

nsMyComponent::nsMyComponent() {}

nsMyComponent::~nsMyComponent(void) {}

nsresult nsMyComponent::Create(const nsIID& aIID, void** aInstancePtr) {
  RefPtr<nsMyComponent> component = new nsMyComponent();
  return component->QueryInterface(aIID, aInstancePtr);
}

// Implementation of nsIObserverService methods

NS_IMETHODIMP
nsMyComponent::AddObserver(nsIObserver* aObserver, const char* aTopic,
                           bool aOwnsWeak) {
  return NS_OK;
}

NS_IMETHODIMP
nsMyComponent::RemoveObserver(nsIObserver* aObserver, const char* aTopic) {
  return NS_OK;
}

NS_IMETHODIMP
nsMyComponent::EnumerateObservers(const char* aTopic,
                                  nsISimpleEnumerator** anEnumerator) {
  return NS_OK;
}

NS_IMETHODIMP
nsMyComponent::NotifyObservers(nsISupports* aSubject, const char* aTopic,
                               const char16_t* aSomeData) {
  return NS_OK;
}
